name:S‚ÄçH‚Äçx‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçz‚Äçi
info:Family Room

info:Family
info:24 Reviews

posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:Except that it is a little expensive, there are no disadvantages, haha
The hotel is next to the Xizha Scenic Area in Wuzhen. Both Wucun Hotel and Daoshe Hotel have shuttle buses to Xizha Scenic Area. If you don't go out from the front, you don't need to apply for facial recognition, you can use the wristband
If you drive, navigate to the Wucun Sales Center. After stopping, there will be staff to help with the luggage, and then take the battery car to the "Village Committee", which is the lobby. After checking in, you have to wait until the afternoon to enter the room, but it doesn't matter. You can make an appoin**ent for all the activities you want to participate in at the front desk first, and then you can start each activity with the wristband
The room is very small, really small, haha, I want to complain about the shower, it is not very convenient to use, it is very hot, you have to bend the faucet to the cold water direction across the center line, it is still a little hot, the water is also very small, and finally I found that I had to open it a little harder, it would be a little better, but the water volume is still not large.
If it is an all-inclusive package, it includes breakfast, lunch and dinner. Compared with the previous comments, the meals feel much better (maybe the expectations are lowered, hahaha), and they are still quite rich. The rice balls, fish porridge and mutton noodles for breakfast are highly recommended. I personally think that lunch is also very special. Although there are no big dishes, they are all dishes that can go well with rice. Bullfrog, stewed beef, Hainanese chicken rice, steamed spareribs with black bean sauce are all delicious. There are small mangoes as fruits, which is great. Dinner has salmon and boiled shrimp, which are also very good. I recommend it. . .
There are many activities. I arrived at 9 o'clock in the morning and played until 4 o'clock in the afternoon of the next day. The full arrangement for 2 days, archery, boating, fishing, picking loquats, feeding silkworms, grinding soy milk, making tofu, climbing trees, making cakes, eating snacks, drinking afternoon tea, eating desserts, and there is a bonfire party in the evening. . . . It's simply too much to play
One more thing to complain about is the amusement facilities area in the children's play center. The lighting feels a bit dim and a bit shabby. The air conditioning in the baking classroom is too cold because they have to ensure the ingredients. There are children outside who are naturally sweating. If they come in to make cakes, they may catch a cold
Overall, it is very, very, very good. The children are already looking forward to coming again next time

msg:During the May Day holiday, I took my daughter to Wucun for a trip. I thought it would be similar to the experience of ancient towns such as Xitang and Nanxun. I didn't expect that Wucun's design is unique. All the groups are original buildings, but the interior has been modified. It has both traditional Jiangnan water village style and modern comfort elements, giving people a unique feeling of both ancient and modern.
In the resort, we tasted a variety of snacks and desserts, each of which was memorable. The sweetness of the desserts was moderate and not greasy, while the snacks were delicious and very suitable for my daughter and me. While enjoying the food, we can also enjoy the beautiful scenery in the resort, as if we were in a painting of Jiangnan water village.
In addition to the food and scenery, the resort's service is also first-class. From check-in to check-out, every detail reflects Wucun's care and concern for guests, especially the rubber boat activity we participated in. The shark coach was very responsible. He not only patiently taught us how to row, but also always paid attention to our safety, allowing us to spend a wonderful afternoon in a relaxed, happy and safe a**osphere.
What surprised me even more was that we were given a pass to the Xizha Scenic Area when we checked into Wu Village. Taking advantage of this opportunity, I took my daughter to visit the beautiful Xizha Scenic Area and felt the unique charm of the Jiangnan Water Village.
During the tour, we unexpectedly discovered a new hotel, the Di Shang Hotel (later found out that it was very close from Wu Village). The new hotel has an elegant environment. We visited the hotel's infinity pool. The design of the pool is very clever, integrating with the canal and the scenery of the entire Xizha, allowing swimmers to feel as if they were in nature. The on-site manager Xiao Wu enthusiastically introduced the hotel's facilities to us and personally took us to experience the singing bowl therapy. The sound of the singing bowl was deep and melodious, making us feel unprecedented relaxation and tranquility.
After experiencing the singing bowl, I became very interested in the new hotel in this scenic area. Next time I come to Wu Village, I may consider booking a room here.
I believe that in the days to come, we will return to this beautiful town again to feel the endless charm it brings us.

msg:I wanted to take advantage of the Qingming holiday to go to Wuzhen. After checking, I decided to stay in the scenic area. Because the departure time was uncertain, I looked for several hotels before I finally found this hotel with a room type that could be cancelled for free before 18:00 on the same day. I chose a package for two adults and one child, two days and one night, all-inclusive (I later found out that all-inclusive was really good). A few days before departure, the hotel staff CCO Xiao Fu came to add WeChat to inform me of the hotel's activities, catering and other related information, as well as how to book activities on the mini program. He was still answering my questions after 11 o'clock in the evening üòÖ. When I just checked into the room, it felt a bit simple. It was the style of a self-built house in the countryside. I guess it might be renovated from the old house of local residents, but the sanitary conditions were in place. The children were equipped with children's toothbrushes and slippers. The toiletries and toilet paper were all brand new and unopened. The free drinks, tea bags, and mineral water were sufficient. The package I booked includes 1 breakfast, 2 meals, tickets to Xizha Scenic Area, and tickets to Wucun. When checking in, everyone was given a wristband (I guess the wristband is for guests who booked the all-inclusive package? Not sure). With the wristband, you can enter and exit Xizha Scenic Area and Wucun Scenic Area unlimited times. At the same time, there are five snack shops in Wucun that are free for wristband customers (Mofang Food Time, Village Tea House, Taoyuan Dessert Shop, Zhiqing Coffee Bar, Daoshe Maiyu Lobby Bar), and you can enjoy it unlimited times. Just look at the business hours of each store on the mini program. As long as you can eat, you can eat from morning to night. It is really friendly to foodies. An additional midnight snack was also given, which was enjoyed at the Zhiqing Generation Restaurant. Most activities in Wucun are also free for wristband customers. Feeding small animals, slides in the children's playhouse, rock climbing, bowling, building blocks, etc. are children's favorites. There are also cycling, KTV, gyms, chess and card rooms, etc. You need to look at the opening hours of the activities and whether reservations are required on the mini program. When I checked out at 12:00 the next day, I was given a small bag of rice as a souvenir. The bracelet did not need to be returned immediately. Except for not being able to enter the room, I could still enjoy all other services until I had enough fun and returned it. Although it was sunny and cloudy these two days, and it drizzled from time to time, I was in a sunny and happy mood. It was a good experience.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom - with View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted February 23, 2024
msg:The room is in the rice warehouse. Wucun is indeed a big village. Now places like rice warehouse and wine alley that don't look like residences have been transformed into rooms.
The rice warehouse accommodation has two floors. I was on the first floor. The advantage is that there is a small courtyard where I can sit and drink tea and overlook the field scenery. It should be considered very leisurely. , of course you can also imagine summer bugs.
The room is actually not big, but a bit narrow. It may have been renovated from an old house, so the sound insulation is average, and you can feel the movement upstairs. The door lock also has a very old key. Staying in winter, there is heating, which is very considerate. The TV cannot be cast, but there are many channels. The Xizha accommodation has uniform toiletries, nightgowns, and children's toothbrushes.
There are two accommodations in Wucun, and one is a rice house. I feel that the rice house is more modern overall, while Wucun Hotel is more original. The breakfasts of both hotels are at Qiangwei Restaurant (can‚Äôt remember the specific name), which is actually not far away.
The breakfast seems quite rich, but I feel like there are not many options. Everyone is eating tofu curd, spicy soup and so on spontaneously. Maybe there is nothing else to eat. There are plenty of Western salads, children's meals, and various pastries.
For dinner, I ate at the Educated Youth Restaurant in Wucun. My mother thought it was quite unpalatable. Although it was very rich, it had no flavor or distinctiveness. Went during the Spring Festival and it seemed like they only had set menus.
I heard from people who bought the all-inclusive package that there were very few food options, so I didn‚Äôt want to eat any more the next day.
There are actually good restaurants in Xizha, so it is better to consider going to Xizha or going out to the scenic spots to eat (the price/performance ratio is still too low).
Another thing about Wucun and Xizha that is suitable for the elderly and children is that there are many browsing cars in the scenic area, but the queues can be quite uncomfortable when there are many people or during peak periods. Especially different buses (for example, some buses only run within Wucun, and some Xizha buses do not go to Wucun) and different stops, it is easy for tourists to get confused. Fortunately, the service is very good, and there are people in each hotel to help coordinate the transportation issues.
